Rose:Button("奇葩飞行", function()
local Players = game:GetService("Players")
local UserInputService = game:GetService("UserInputService")
local RunService = game:GetService("RunService")
local TweenService = game:GetService("TweenService")
local Workspace = game:GetService("Workspace")

-- 确保使用正确的玩家对象
local player = Players.LocalPlayer

-- 初始化角色变量
local character = player.Character or player.CharacterAdded:Wait()
local humanoid = character:WaitForChild("Humanoid")
local rootPart = character:WaitForChild("HumanoidRootPart")

-- 飞行状态
local isFlying = false
local flightSpeed = 50
local maxSpeed = 150
local boostMultiplier = 2.5
local isBoosting = false
local flightHeight = 5
local isMobile = UserInputService.TouchEnabled

-- 更真实的超人飞行动画
local flightAnimation = Instance.new("Animation")
flightAnimation.AnimationId = "rbxassetid://188647419" -- 更标准的超人飞行动画

-- 存储原始关节角度（用于恢复）
local originalJoints = {}

-- 粒子效果
local function createFlightEffects()
    local effects = {}
    
    -- 脚部粒子
    local leftFoot = character:FindFirstChild("LeftFoot") or character:FindFirstChild("LeftLeg") or rootPart
    local rightFoot = character:FindFirstChild("RightFoot") or character:FindFirstChild("RightLeg") or rootPart
    
    if leftFoot then
        local leftParticle = Instance.new("ParticleEmitter")
        leftParticle.Color = ColorSequence.new(Color3.new(0, 0.8, 1))
        leftParticle.LightEmission = 0.8
        leftParticle.Size = NumberSequence.new(0.5)
        leftParticle.Texture = "rbxassetid://242019837"
        leftParticle.Transparency = NumberSequence.new(0.5)
        leftParticle.Lifetime = NumberRange.new(0.5)
        leftParticle.Rate = 50
        leftParticle.Speed = NumberRange.new(5)
        leftParticle.VelocitySpread = 30
        leftParticle.Parent = leftFoot
        table.insert(effects, leftParticle)
    end
    
    if rightFoot then
        local rightParticle = Instance.new("ParticleEmitter")
        rightParticle.Color = ColorSequence.new(Color3.new(0, 0.8, 1))
        rightParticle.LightEmission = 0.8
        rightParticle.Size = NumberSequence.new(0.5)
        rightParticle.Texture = "rbxassetid://242019837"
        rightParticle.Transparency = NumberSequence.new(0.5)
        rightParticle.Lifetime = NumberRange.new(0.5)
        rightParticle.Rate = 50
        rightParticle.Speed = NumberRange.new(5)
        rightParticle.VelocitySpread = 30
        rightParticle.Parent = rightFoot
        table.insert(effects, rightParticle)
    end
    
    -- 音效
    local flightSound = Instance.new("Sound")
    flightSound.SoundId = "rbxassetid://130977847"
    flightSound.Volume = 0.7
    flightSound.Looped = true
    flightSound.Parent = rootPart
    flightSound:Play()
    table.insert(effects, flightSound)
    
    return effects
end

-- 保存原始关节配置
local function saveOriginalJoints()
    originalJoints = {}
    
    local function saveJoint(jointName)
        local joint = character:FindFirstChild(jointName, true)
        if joint and joint:IsA("Motor6D") then
            originalJoints[jointName] = {
                C0 = joint.C0,
                C1 = joint.C1
            }
        end
    end
    
    saveJoint("Root")
    saveJoint("Neck")
    saveJoint("Waist")
    saveJoint("Left Shoulder")
    saveJoint("Right Shoulder")
    saveJoint("Left Hip")
    saveJoint("Right Hip")
end

-- 姿势修复核心函数（完全重构）
local function forceSupermanPose()
    if not character or not humanoid then return end
    
    -- 完全禁用物理模拟和干扰状态
    humanoid.PlatformStand = true
    humanoid.AutoRotate = false
    
    -- 禁用所有可能影响姿势的状态
    for _, state in ipairs(Enum.HumanoidStateType:GetEnumItems()) do
        if state ~= Enum.HumanoidStateType.Flying then
            humanoid:SetStateEnabled(state, false)
        end
    end
    
    -- 强制设置姿势状态
    humanoid:ChangeState(Enum.HumanoidStateType.Flying)
    
    -- 应用自定义姿势
    local torso = character:FindFirstChild("UpperTorso") or character:FindFirstChild("Torso")
    if not torso then return end
    
    -- 身体水平飞行姿势 (90度前倾)
    local rootJoint = torso:FindFirstChild("Root") or torso:FindFirstChild("Waist")
    if rootJoint and rootJoint:IsA("Motor6D") then
        rootJoint.C0 = CFrame.new(0, 0, 0) * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(-90), 0, 0)
    end
    
    -- 手臂向前伸直
    local leftShoulder = torso:FindFirstChild("Left Shoulder") or torso:FindFirstChild("LeftShoulder")
    if leftShoulder and leftShoulder:IsA("Motor6D") then
        leftShoulder.C0 = CFrame.new(-1, 0.5, 0) * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(-20), math.rad(-90), math.rad(-10))
    end
    
    local rightShoulder = torso:FindFirstChild("Right Shoulder") or torso:FindFirstChild("RightShoulder")
    if rightShoulder and rightShoulder:IsA("Motor6D") then
        rightShoulder.C0 = CFrame.new(1, 0.5, 0) * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(-20), math.rad(90), math.rad(10))
    end
    
    -- 腿部并拢向后伸直
    local leftHip = torso:FindFirstChild("Left Hip") or torso:FindFirstChild("LeftHip")
    if leftHip and leftHip:IsA("Motor6D") then
        leftHip.C0 = CFrame.new(-1, -1, 0) * CFrame.Angles(0, math.rad(-90), 0)
    end
    
    local rightHip = torso:FindFirstChild("Right Hip") or torso:FindFirstChild("RightHip")
    if rightHip and rightHip:IsA("Motor6D") then
        rightHip.C0 = CFrame.new(1, -1, 0) * CFrame.Angles(0, math.rad(90), 0)
    end
    
    -- 头部向前看
    local neck = torso:FindFirstChild("Neck") or character:FindFirstChild("Neck")
    if neck and neck:IsA("Motor6D") then
        neck.C0 = CFrame.new(0, 1, 0) * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(-20), 0, 0)
    end
end

-- 恢复原始姿势
local function restoreOriginalPose()
    for jointName, data in pairs(originalJoints) do
        local joint = character:FindFirstChild(jointName, true)
        if joint and joint:IsA("Motor6D") then
            joint.C0 = data.C0
            joint.C1 = data.C1
        end
    end
end

-- 飞行姿势控制
local flightTrack
local function setFlightPose(enable)
    if not character or not humanoid then return end
    
    if enable then
        -- 保存原始关节配置
        saveOriginalJoints()
        
        -- 加载飞行动画
        local animator = humanoid:FindFirstChildOfClass("Animator")
        if animator then
            flightTrack = animator:LoadAnimation(flightAnimation)
            flightTrack.Looped = true
            flightTrack.Priority = Enum.AnimationPriority.Action
            flightTrack:Play()
        end
        
        -- 强制应用超人姿势
        forceSupermanPose()
    else
        -- 停止动画
        if flightTrack then
            flightTrack:Stop()
            flightTrack:Destroy()
            flightTrack = nil
        end
        
        -- 恢复原始姿势
        restoreOriginalPose()
        
        -- 恢复状态
        humanoid.PlatformStand = false
        humanoid.AutoRotate = true
        
        -- 重新启用状态
        for _, state in ipairs(Enum.HumanoidStateType:GetEnumItems()) do
            humanoid:SetStateEnabled(state, true)
        end
    end
end

-- 创建移动设备控制UI - 优化版
local mobileControls
local function createMobileControls()
    local screenGui = Instance.new("ScreenGui")
    screenGui.Name = "FlightMobileControls"
    screenGui.ResetOnSpawn = false
    screenGui.Parent = player:WaitForChild("PlayerGui")
    
    -- 控制容器（用于整体缩放）
    local controlsContainer = Instance.new("Frame")
    controlsContainer.Name = "ControlsContainer"
    controlsContainer.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 1, 0)
    controlsContainer.BackgroundTransparency = 1
    controlsContainer.Parent = screenGui
    
    -- 虚拟摇杆 (左下角)
    local joystickOuter = Instance.new("Frame")
    joystickOuter.Name = "JoystickOuter"
    joystickOuter.Size = UDim2.new(0.2, 0, 0.2, 0)
    joystickOuter.Position = UDim2.new(0.05, 0, 0.75, 0)
    joystickOuter.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.new(0.2, 0.2, 0.2)
    joystickOuter.BackgroundTransparency = 0.5
    joystickOuter.BorderSizePixel = 0
    joystickOuter.Parent = controlsContainer
    
    local corner = Instance.new("UICorner")
    corner.CornerRadius = UDim.new(1, 0)
    corner.Parent = joystickOuter
    
    local joystickInner = Instance.new("Frame")
    joystickInner.Name = "JoystickInner"
    joystickInner.Size = UDim2.new(0.4, 0, 0.4, 0)
    joystickInner.AnchorPoint = Vector2.new(0.5, 0.5)
    joystickInner.Position = UDim2.new(0.5, 0, 0.5, 0)
    joystickInner.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.new(1, 1, 1)
    joystickInner.BackgroundTransparency = 0.7
    joystickInner.BorderSizePixel = 0
    joystickInner.Parent = joystickOuter
    
    local cornerInner = Instance.new("UICorner")
    cornerInner.CornerRadius = UDim.new(1, 0)
    cornerInner.Parent = joystickInner
    
    -- 摇杆标签
    local joystickLabel = Instance.new("TextLabel")
    joystickLabel.Name = "JoystickLabel"
    joystickLabel.Text = "移动"
    joystickLabel.TextColor3 = Color3.new(1, 1, 1)
    joystickLabel.TextSize = 16
    joystickLabel.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0.2, 0)
    joystickLabel.Position = UDim2.new(0, 0, -0.2, 0)
    joystickLabel.BackgroundTransparency = 1
    joystickLabel.Parent = joystickOuter
    
    -- 垂直控制摇杆 (右下角)
    local verticalJoystickOuter = Instance.new("Frame")
    verticalJoystickOuter.Name = "VerticalJoystickOuter"
    verticalJoystickOuter.Size = UDim2.new(0.15, 0, 0.2, 0)
    verticalJoystickOuter.Position = UDim2.new(0.85, 0, 0.75, 0)
    verticalJoystickOuter.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.new(0.2, 0.2, 0.2)
    verticalJoystickOuter.BackgroundTransparency = 0.5
    verticalJoystickOuter.BorderSizePixel = 0
    verticalJoystickOuter.Parent = controlsContainer
    
    local vCorner = Instance.new("UICorner")
    vCorner.CornerRadius = UDim.new(1, 0)
    vCorner.Parent = verticalJoystickOuter
    
    local verticalJoystickInner = Instance.new("Frame")
    verticalJoystickInner.Name = "VerticalJoystickInner"
    verticalJoystickInner.Size = UDim2.new(0.4, 0, 0.4, 0)
    verticalJoystickInner.AnchorPoint = Vector2.new(0.5, 0.5)
    verticalJoystickInner.Position = UDim2.new(0.5, 0, 0.5, 0)
    verticalJoystickInner.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.new(1, 1, 1)
    verticalJoystickInner.BackgroundTransparency = 0.7
    verticalJoystickInner.BorderSizePixel = 0
    verticalJoystickInner.Parent = verticalJoystickOuter
    
    local vCornerInner = Instance.new("UICorner")
    vCornerInner.CornerRadius = UDim.new(1, 0)
    vCornerInner.Parent = verticalJoystickInner
    
    -- 垂直摇杆标签
    local verticalLabel = Instance.new("TextLabel")
    verticalLabel.Name = "VerticalLabel"
    verticalLabel.Text = "高度"
    verticalLabel.TextColor3 = Color3.new(1, 1, 1)
    verticalLabel.TextSize = 16
    verticalLabel.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0.2, 0)
    verticalLabel.Position = UDim2.new(0, 0, -0.2, 0)
    verticalLabel.BackgroundTransparency = 1
    verticalLabel.Parent = verticalJoystickOuter
    
    -- 加速按钮 (右下角)
    local boostButton = Instance.new("TextButton")
    boostButton.Name = "BoostButton"
    boostButton.Size = UDim2.new(0.2, 0, 0.1, 0)
    boostButton.Position = UDim2.new(0.75, 0, 0.85, 0)
    boostButton.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.new(1, 0.5, 0)
    boostButton.BackgroundTransparency = 0.5
    boostButton.Text = "加速"
    boostButton.TextSize = 18
    boostButton.TextColor3 = Color3.new(1, 1, 1)
    boostButton.Parent = controlsContainer
    
    -- 加速按钮圆角
    local boostCorner = Instance.new("UICorner")
    boostCorner.CornerRadius = UDim.new(0.3, 0)
    boostCorner.Parent = boostButton
    
    -- 飞行开关按钮 (顶部中央)
    local flightToggleButton = Instance.new("TextButton")
    flightToggleButton.Name = "FlightToggleButton"
    flightToggleButton.Size = UDim2.new(0.3, 0, 0.08, 0)
    flightToggleButton.Position = UDim2.new(0.35, 0, 0.05, 0)
    flightToggleButton.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.new(0, 0.6, 1)
    flightToggleButton.BackgroundTransparency = 0.5
    flightToggleButton.Text = "开始飞行"
    flightToggleButton.TextSize = 20
    flightToggleButton.TextColor3 = Color3.new(1, 1, 1)
    flightToggleButton.Parent = controlsContainer
    
    -- 飞行按钮圆角
    local flightCorner = Instance.new("UICorner")
    flightCorner.CornerRadius = UDim.new(0.2, 0)
    flightCorner.Parent = flightToggleButton
    
    -- 摇杆数据结构
    local virtualJoystick = {
        Outer = joystickOuter,
        Inner = joystickInner,
        Active = false,
        Position = Vector2.new(0,0),
        StartPos = nil
    }
    
    local verticalJoystick = {
        Outer = verticalJoystickOuter,
        Inner = verticalJoystickInner,
        Active = false,
        Position = Vector2.new(0,0),
        StartPos = nil
    }
    
    -- 摇杆事件
    joystickOuter.InputBegan:Connect(function(input)
        if input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Touch then
            virtualJoystick.Active = true
            virtualJoystick.StartPos = Vector2.new(input.Position.X, input.Position.Y)
        end
    end)
    
    joystickOuter.InputChanged:Connect(function(input)
        if virtualJoystick.Active and input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Touch then
            local currentPos = Vector2.new(input.Position.X, input.Position.Y)
            local delta = currentPos - virtualJoystick.StartPos
            local maxRadius = joystickOuter.AbsoluteSize.X / 2
            local magnitude = math.min(delta.Magnitude, maxRadius)
            local direction = delta.Unit
            
            virtualJoystick.Position = direction * magnitude / maxRadius
            joystickInner.Position = UDim2.new(0.5, direction.X * magnitude, 0.5, direction.Y * magnitude)
        end
    end)
    
    joystickOuter.InputEnded:Connect(function(input)
        if input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Touch then
            virtualJoystick.Active = false
            virtualJoystick.Position = Vector2.new(0,0)
            joystickInner.Position = UDim2.new(0.5,0,0.5,0)
        end
    end)
    
    -- 垂直摇杆事件
    verticalJoystickOuter.InputBegan:Connect(function(input)
        if input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Touch then
            verticalJoystick.Active = true
            verticalJoystick.StartPos = Vector2.new(input.Position.X, input.Position.Y)
        end
    end)
    
    verticalJoystickOuter.InputChanged:Connect(function(input)
        if verticalJoystick.Active and input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Touch then
            local currentPos = Vector2.new(input.Position.X, input.Position.Y)
            local delta = currentPos - verticalJoystick.StartPos
            local maxRadius = verticalJoystickOuter.AbsoluteSize.Y / 2
            local magnitude = math.min(delta.Magnitude, maxRadius)
            local direction = delta.Unit
            
            -- 只取Y轴移动
            verticalJoystick.Position = Vector2.new(0, direction.Y * magnitude / maxRadius)
            verticalJoystickInner.Position = UDim2.new(0.5, 0, 0.5, direction.Y * magnitude)
        end
    end)
    
    verticalJoystickOuter.InputEnded:Connect(function(input)
        if input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Touch then
            verticalJoystick.Active = false
            verticalJoystick.Position = Vector2.new(0,0)
            verticalJoystickInner.Position = UDim2.new(0.5,0,0.5,0)
        end
    end)
    
    -- 按钮事件
    local boostActive = false
    
    boostButton.MouseButton1Down:Connect(function()
        boostActive = true
        boostButton.BackgroundTransparency = 0.2
    end)
    
    boostButton.MouseButton1Up:Connect(function()
        boostActive = false
        boostButton.BackgroundTransparency = 0.5
    end)
    
    -- 返回控制对象
    return {
        joystick = virtualJoystick,
        verticalJoystick = verticalJoystick,
        boostActive = function() return boostActive end,
        toggleButton = flightToggleButton
    }
end

-- 如果设备是移动设备，创建移动控制
if isMobile then
    mobileControls = createMobileControls()
end

-- 飞行控制核心
local flightConnection
local flightEffects = {}
local function startFlying()
    if isFlying then return end
    isFlying = true
    
    -- 获取当前角色
    character = player.Character
    humanoid = character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
    rootPart = character:WaitForChild("HumanoidRootPart")
    
    if not character or not humanoid or not rootPart then
        warn("无法启动飞行：角色部件缺失")
        isFlying = false
        return
    end
    
    -- 设置超人姿势（立即应用）
    setFlightPose(true)
    
    -- 创建粒子效果
    flightEffects = createFlightEffects()
    
    -- 飞行循环
    flightConnection = RunService.Heartbeat:Connect(function(delta)
        if not character or not rootPart or not humanoid or not isFlying then
            if flightConnection then
                flightConnection:Disconnect()
            end
            return
        end
        
        -- 姿势保护：防止其他动作干扰
        forceSupermanPose()
        
        -- 获取相机方向
        local camera = Workspace.CurrentCamera
        if not camera then return end
        
        local cameraCFrame = camera.CFrame
        local lookVector = cameraCFrame.LookVector
        local rightVector = cameraCFrame.RightVector
        local upVector = Vector3.new(0, 1, 0)
        
        -- 计算移动方向
        local direction = Vector3.new()
        
        if isMobile and mobileControls then
            -- 移动设备控制 - 新版
            local joyPos = mobileControls.joystick.Position
            direction = direction + lookVector * joyPos.Y
            direction = direction + rightVector * joyPos.X
            
            -- 垂直控制
            local verticalPos = mobileControls.verticalJoystick.Position.Y
            direction = direction + upVector * verticalPos
            
            -- 加速控制
            isBoosting = mobileControls.boostActive()
        else
            -- 电脑控制
            if UserInputService:IsKeyDown(Enum.KeyCode.W) then
                direction = direction + lookVector
            end
            
            if UserInputService:IsKeyDown(Enum.KeyCode.S) then
                direction = direction - lookVector
            end
            
            if UserInputService:IsKeyDown(Enum.KeyCode.D) then
                direction = direction + rightVector
            end
            
            if UserInputService:IsKeyDown(Enum.KeyCode.A) then
                direction = direction - rightVector
            end
            
            if UserInputService:IsKeyDown(Enum.KeyCode.Space) then
                direction = direction + upVector
            end
            
            if UserInputService:IsKeyDown(Enum.KeyCode.LeftControl) then
                direction = direction - upVector
            end
            
            isBoosting = UserInputService:IsKeyDown(Enum.KeyCode.LeftShift)
        end
        
        -- 加速控制
        local currentSpeed = isBoosting and flightSpeed * boostMultiplier or flightSpeed
        currentSpeed = math.min(currentSpeed, maxSpeed)
        
        -- 应用移动
        if direction.Magnitude > 0 then
            direction = direction.Unit * currentSpeed
            
            -- 关键修复：正确应用速度
            rootPart.Velocity = Vector3.new(direction.X, direction.Y, direction.Z)
            
            -- 保持超人姿势方向
            local targetCFrame = CFrame.new(rootPart.Position, rootPart.Position + lookVector)
            rootPart.CFrame = targetCFrame
        else
            -- 悬停时保持位置
            rootPart.Velocity = Vector3.new(0, 0, 0)
        end
    end)
end

-- 停止飞行
local function stopFlying()
    if not isFlying then return end
    isFlying = false
    
    -- 恢复姿势
    setFlightPose(false)
    
    -- 移除效果
    for _, effect in ipairs(flightEffects) do
        effect:Destroy()
    end
    flightEffects = {}
    
    -- 停止循环
    if flightConnection then
        flightConnection:Disconnect()
    end
    
    -- 重置速度
    if rootPart then
        rootPart.Velocity = Vector3.new(0, 0, 0)
    end
    
    -- 恢复重力
    if humanoid then
        humanoid.PlatformStand = false
    end
end

-- 飞行开关函数
local function toggleFlight()
    if isFlying then
        stopFlying()
        if isMobile and mobileControls and mobileControls.toggleButton then
            mobileControls.toggleButton.Text = "开始飞行"
            mobileControls.toggleButton.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.new(0, 0.6, 1)
        end
    else
        startFlying()
        if isMobile and mobileControls and mobileControls.toggleButton then
            mobileControls.toggleButton.Text = "停止飞行"
            mobileControls.toggleButton.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.new(1, 0.2, 0.2)
        end
    end
end

-- 移动设备按钮绑定
if isMobile and mobileControls and mobileControls.toggleButton then
    mobileControls.toggleButton.Activated:Connect(function()
        toggleFlight()
    end)
end

-- 电脑设备按键绑定
if not isMobile then
    UserInputService.InputBegan:Connect(function(input, gameProcessed)
        if gameProcessed then return end
        
        -- 切换飞行状态 (F键)
        if input.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.F then
            toggleFlight()
        end
    end)
end

-- 角色重生时重置
player.CharacterAdded:Connect(function(newChar)
    character = newChar
    humanoid = newChar:WaitForChild("Humanoid")
    rootPart = newChar:WaitForChild("HumanoidRootPart")
    
    -- 停止当前飞行
    stopFlying()
    
    -- 重新创建移动设备控制UI
    if isMobile then
        if mobileControls then
            -- 清理旧UI
            local controlsContainer = player.PlayerGui:FindFirstChild("FlightMobileControls")
            if controlsContainer then
                controlsContainer:Destroy()
            end
        end
        mobileControls = createMobileControls()
        if mobileControls and mobileControls.toggleButton then
            mobileControls.toggleButton.Activated:Connect(toggleFlight)
        end
    end
end)

flightIndicator.BorderSizePixel = 0
flightIndicator.Visible = false

-- 更新UI
RunService.Heartbeat:Connect(function()
    if isFlying and rootPart then
        flightIndicator.Visible = true
        statusText.Text = isBoosting and "飞行模式: 加速中!" or "飞行模式: 开启"
        statusText.TextColor3 = isBoosting and Color3.new(1, 0.5, 0) or Color3.new(0.5, 1, 1)
        
        -- 更新速度指示器
        local currentSpeed = math.min(rootPart.Velocity.Magnitude, maxSpeed)
        local fillPercent = currentSpeed / maxSpeed
        speedFill.Size = UDim2.new(fillPercent, 0, 1, 0)
        speedFill.BackgroundColor3 = isBoosting and Color3.new(1, 0.7, 0.2) or Color3.new(0.2, 0.8, 1)
    else
        flightIndicator.Visible = false
    end
end)

-- 初始状态
flightIndicator.Visible = false

-- 添加一个启动消息
print("超人飞行脚本已加载完成！按F键（电脑）或点击开始飞行按钮（手机）启动。")
end)
Rose:Button("半无敌(无法关闭)", function()
local Players = game:GetService("Players")
local RunService = game:GetService("RunService")

-- 获取本地玩家
local player = Players.LocalPlayer
local character = player.Character or player.CharacterAdded:Wait()
local humanoid = character:WaitForChild("Humanoid")
local rootPart = character:WaitForChild("HumanoidRootPart")

-- 核心无敌功能
local function applyUltimateImmunity()
    -- 1. 完全移除伤害碰撞箱
    for _, part in ipairs(character:GetDescendants()) do
        if part:IsA("BasePart") then
            -- 禁用所有物理碰撞
            part.CanCollide = false
            part.CanTouch = false
            part.CanQuery = false
            part.Massless = true
        end
    end

    -- 2. 免疫掉落伤害
    if humanoid:GetState() ~= Enum.HumanoidStateType.Ragdoll then
        humanoid:SetStateEnabled(Enum.HumanoidStateType.Ragdoll, false)
    end
    
    -- 3. 核心免疫函数
    local function healthLock()
        -- 防止角色死亡
        if humanoid.Health <= 0 then
            humanoid:ChangeState(Enum.HumanoidStateType.Running)
        end
        
        -- 锁定生命值
        humanoid.Health = humanoid.MaxHealth
        
        -- 移除所有负面效果
        for _, effect in ipairs(humanoid:GetChildren()) do
            if effect:IsA("StringValue") and effect.Name:match("KO") then
                effect:Destroy()
            end
        end
        
        -- 重置下落伤害缓冲
        if rootPart then
            rootPart.Velocity = Vector3.new(rootPart.Velocity.X, math.min(rootPart.Velocity.Y, 0), rootPart.Velocity.Z)
        end
    end
    
    -- 4. 物理接触防护
    local touchIgnored = {}
    for _, part in ipairs(character:GetDescendants()) do
        if part:IsA("BasePart") then
            -- 拦截所有触碰事件
            part.Touched:Connect(function(otherPart)
                if not touchIgnored[otherPart] then
                    touchIgnored[otherPart] = true
                    otherPart.CanCollide = false
                    otherPart.CanTouch = false
                end
            end)
        end
    end
    
    -- 5. 创建防护连接
    local heartbeatConnection = RunService.Heartbeat:Connect(healthLock)
    
    return heartbeatConnection
end

-- 主功能应用
local immunityConnection = applyUltimateImmunity()

-- 角色重生时重新应用
player.CharacterAdded:Connect(function(newCharacter)
    character = newCharacter
    humanoid = newCharacter:WaitForChild("Humanoid")
    rootPart = newCharacter:WaitForChild("HumanoidRootPart")
    
    -- 移除旧防护
    if immunityConnection then
        immunityConnection:Disconnect()
    end
    
    -- 等待物理加载
    task.wait(0.5)
    
    -- 应用新防护
    immunityConnection = applyUltimateImmunity()
    
    print("无敌系统已更新: 角色重生保护生效")
end)

-- 自我修复机制
RunService.Heartbeat:Connect(function()
    -- 确保连接有效
    if immunityConnection and immunityConnection.Connected ~= true then
        immunityConnection = applyUltimateImmunity()
    end
    
    -- 强制免疫所有接触
    if character then
        for _, item in ipairs(workspace:GetDescendants()) do
            if item:IsA("BasePart") and not item:IsDescendantOf(character) then
                item.CanCollide = false
                item.CanTouch = false
            end
        end
    end
end)

print("终极无敌系统激活成功！")
print("状态: 无敌模式 | 免疫接触 | 无掉落伤害 | 无视秒杀")

local Players = game:GetService("Players")
local RunService = game:GetService("RunService")
local UserInputService = game:GetService("UserInputService")
local Workspace = game:GetService("Workspace")

-- 确保使用正确的玩家对象
local player = Players.LocalPlayer

-- 初始化角色变量
local character = player.Character or player.CharacterAdded:Wait()
local humanoid = character:WaitForChild("Humanoid")
local rootPart = character:WaitForChild("HumanoidRootPart")

-- 增强伤害免疫系统
local function setupAbsoluteDamageImmunity()
    -- 1. 完全禁用死亡状态
    humanoid:SetStateEnabled(Enum.HumanoidStateType.Dead, false)
    
    -- 2. 拦截所有伤害事件
    local function interceptDamage()
        -- 移除所有伤害接收器
        for _, connection in ipairs(getconnections(humanoid.Changed)) do
            if connection.Function and debug.info(connection.Function, "n") == "takeDamage" then
                connection:Disable()
            end
        end
        
        -- 替换TakeDamage方法
        if humanoid:FindFirstChild("TakeDamage") then
            humanoid.TakeDamage:Connect(function(damage)
                return 0  -- 抵消所有伤害
            end)
        else
            -- 创建自定义TakeDamage事件
            local takeDamage = Instance.new("BindableEvent")
            takeDamage.Name = "TakeDamage"
            takeDamage.Parent = humanoid
            
            humanoid.TakeDamage = takeDamage.Event
            
            takeDamage.Event:Connect(function(damage)
                return 0
            end)
        end
    end
    
    -- 3. 生命值锁定系统
    local healthLock
    healthLock = RunService.Heartbeat:Connect(function()
        -- 强制锁定生命值为最大值
        humanoid.Health = humanoid.MaxHealth
        
        -- 防止死亡状态
        if humanoid:GetState() == Enum.HumanoidStateType.Dead then
            humanoid:ChangeState(Enum.HumanoidStateType.Running)
        end
    end)
    
    -- 4. 身体部件无敌化
    local function makePartsInvincible()
        for _, part in ipairs(character:GetDescendants()) do
            if part:IsA("BasePart") then
                -- 设置无敌属性
                part:SetAttribute("Invincible", true)
                
                -- 防止物理交互
                part.CanCollide = false
                part.CanTouch = false
                part.CanQuery = false
                part.Massless = true
                
                -- 防止爆炸伤害
                if part:FindFirstChild("Explosive") then
                    part.Explosive:Destroy()
                end
                
                -- 移除所有伤害相关脚本
                for _, script in ipairs(part:GetChildren()) do
                    if script:IsA("Script") and script.Name:find("Damage") then
                        script:Destroy()
                    end
                end
            end
        end
    end
    
    -- 5. 特殊状态防护
    if character:FindFirstChild("BodyEffects") then
        local bodyEffects = character.BodyEffects
        if bodyEffects:FindFirstChild("K.O") then
            bodyEffects["K.O"]:Destroy()
        end
        if bodyEffects:FindFirstChild("Dead") then
            bodyEffects.Dead:Destroy()
        end
    end
    
    -- 应用所有保护
    interceptDamage()
    makePartsInvincible()
    
    return healthLock
end

-- 智能移动系统
local function setupSmartMovement()
    -- 1. 状态管理连接
    local stateConnection
    stateConnection = humanoid.StateChanged:Connect(function(_, newState)
        -- 当角色开始跳跃时
        if newState == Enum.HumanoidStateType.Jumping then
            -- 启用PlatformStand防止摔伤
            humanoid.PlatformStand = true
        end
        
        -- 当角色落地时
        if newState == Enum.HumanoidStateType.Landed then
            -- 立即禁用PlatformStand
            humanoid.PlatformStand = false
            
            -- 强制角色站立
            humanoid:ChangeState(Enum.HumanoidStateType.Running)
        end
    end)
    
    -- 2. 每帧移动恢复系统
    local moveRecoveryConnection
    moveRecoveryConnection = RunService.Heartbeat:Connect(function()
        -- 确保角色能站起来
        if humanoid.FloorMaterial ~= Enum.Material.Air then
            -- 强制禁用PlatformStand
            humanoid.PlatformStand = false
            
            -- 确保角色处于站立状态
            if humanoid:GetState() ~= Enum.HumanoidStateType.Running then
                humanoid:ChangeState(Enum.HumanoidStateType.Running)
            end
            
            -- 重置物理状态
            if rootPart then
                rootPart.AssemblyLinearVelocity = Vector3.new()
                rootPart.AssemblyAngularVelocity = Vector3.new()
            end
        end
    end)
    
    -- 3. 防摔落机制
    local fallProtectionConnection
    fallProtectionConnection = RunService.Heartbeat:Connect(function()
        if rootPart and rootPart.Velocity.Y < -50 then
            -- 限制最大下落速度
            rootPart.Velocity = Vector3.new(rootPart.Velocity.X, math.max(rootPart.Velocity.Y, -20), rootPart.Velocity.Z)
        end
    end)
    
    -- 返回断开函数
    return function()
        if stateConnection then stateConnection:Disconnect() end
        if moveRecoveryConnection then moveRecoveryConnection:Disconnect() end
        if fallProtectionConnection then fallProtectionConnection:Disconnect() end
    end
end

-- 主应用函数
local function applyImmortality()
    if not character or not humanoid or not rootPart then return end
    
    -- 应用伤害免疫
    local healthLock = setupAbsoluteDamageImmunity()
    
    -- 应用智能移动系统
    local disconnectMovement = setupSmartMovement()
    
    -- 返回断开函数
    return function()
        if healthLock then healthLock:Disconnect() end
        if disconnectMovement then disconnectMovement() end
    end
end

-- 应用不死系统
local disconnectImmortality = applyImmortality()

-- 角色重生时重新应用
player.CharacterAdded:Connect(function(newChar)
    character = newChar
    humanoid = newChar:WaitForChild("Humanoid")
    rootPart = newChar:WaitForChild("HumanoidRootPart")
    
    -- 等待角色完全加载
    wait(1)  -- 确保所有组件加载完成
    
    -- 重新应用系统
    if disconnectImmortality then
        disconnectImmortality()
    end
    disconnectImmortality = applyImmortality()
    
    -- 额外延迟确保保护生效
    wait(0.5)
    setupAbsoluteDamageImmunity()
end)

print("终极不死系统已激活！角色现在：")
print("- 完全免疫所有伤害（包括秒杀）")
print("- 高处掉落不会死亡")
print("- 可以正常移动和跳跃")
print("- 落地后立即恢复移动")

-- 持续监控系统
RunService.Heartbeat:Connect(function()
    -- 确保角色始终存在
    if not character or not character.Parent then
        character = player.Character
    end
    
    -- 确保人形始终存在
    if character and not humanoid then
        humanoid = character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
    end
    
    -- 确保根部件始终存在
    if character and not rootPart then
        rootPart = character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
    end
    
    -- 如果保护断开，重新应用
    if not disconnectImmortality or not pcall(disconnectImmortality) then
        disconnectImmortality = applyImmortality()
    end
end)
end)

local Tab114 = Window:Tab("通用8", '5436396975')
local superuniversal9 = Tab114:section("脚本", true)

local Players = game:GetService("Players")
local player = Players.LocalPlayer

-- State
local isRagdolled = false
local motorBackup = {}

local function getCharacter()
    return player.Character or player.CharacterAdded:Wait()
end

-- Ragdoll function
local function toggleRagdoll()
    local character = getCharacter()
    local humanoid = character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
    if not humanoid or humanoid.Health <= 0 then return end

    local root = character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
    if not root then return end

    if not isRagdolled then
        -- Disable humanoid states to allow physics to take over
        humanoid:ChangeState(Enum.HumanoidStateType.Physics)
        humanoid.AutoRotate = false

        -- Store original joints
        motorBackup = {}

        for _, joint in ipairs(character:GetDescendants()) do
            if joint:IsA("Motor6D") then
                local socket = Instance.new("BallSocketConstraint")
                local a1 = Instance.new("Attachment")
                local a2 = Instance.new("Attachment")

                a1.CFrame = joint.C0
                a2.CFrame = joint.C1
                a1.Parent = joint.Part0
                a2.Parent = joint.Part1

                socket.Attachment0 = a1
                socket.Attachment1 = a2
                socket.Parent = joint.Parent
                socket.LimitsEnabled = true
                socket.TwistLimitsEnabled = true

                motorBackup[joint.Name .. "_" .. joint:GetFullName()] = {
                    Part0 = joint.Part0,
                    Part1 = joint.Part1,
                    C0 = joint.C0,
                    C1 = joint.C1,
                    Parent = joint.Parent,
                }

                joint:Destroy()
            end
        end

        -- Make them fall by applying a slight upward velocity first
        root.Velocity = Vector3.new(0, 15, 0)

        isRagdolled = true

    else
        -- Restore motors
        for _, data in pairs(motorBackup) do
            local motor = Instance.new("Motor6D")
            motor.Name = "RestoredMotor"
            motor.Part0 = data.Part0
            motor.Part1 = data.Part1
            motor.C0 = data.C0
            motor.C1 = data.C1
            motor.Parent = data.Parent
        end
        motorBackup = {}

        humanoid:ChangeState(Enum.HumanoidStateType.GettingUp)
        humanoid.AutoRotate = true

        -- Remove leftover attachments/sockets
        for _, item in ipairs(character:GetDescendants()) do
            if item:IsA("BallSocketConstraint") or item:IsA("Attachment") then
                item:Destroy()
            end
        end

        isRagdolled = false
    end
end

-- Revert on respawn
player.CharacterAdded:Connect(function(char)
    isRagdolled = false
    motorBackup = {}
end)

-- 全局通行证开关状态
local gamepassEnabled = false
local originalUserId = game.Players.LocalPlayer.UserId
local originalPlayerHasPass = nil
local hookedRemotes = {}

-- 增强版免费游戏通行证功能
local function enableGamepassHacks()
    -- 方法1: 修改UserId
    if game.CreatorType == Enum.CreatorType.User then
        game.Players.LocalPlayer.UserId = game.CreatorId
    elseif game.CreatorType == Enum.CreatorType.Group then
        game.Players.LocalPlayer.UserId = game:GetService("GroupService"):GetGroupInfoAsync(game.CreatorId).Owner.Id
    end
    
    -- 方法2: 劫持GamePassService
    local gamepassService = game:GetService("GamePassService")
    if not originalPlayerHasPass then
        originalPlayerHasPass = gamepassService.PlayerHasPass
    end
    
    gamepassService.PlayerHasPass = function(_, gamepassId)
        return true -- 总是返回true表示拥有所有通行证
    end
    
    -- 方法3: 拦截远程调用
    local remotesToHook = {
        "GamePassEvent", "GamepassEvent", "GamePass", "PurchaseGamePass", 
        "BuyGamepass", "GamePassManager", "PassEvent", "GamepassPurchase"
    }
    
    for _, name in ipairs(remotesToHook) do
        local remote = game.ReplicatedStorage:FindFirstChild(name)
        if remote and not hookedRemotes[name] then
            if remote:IsA("RemoteEvent") then
                local oldFire = remote.FireServer
                remote.FireServer = function(_, ...)
                    local args = {...}
                    if args[1] == "Purchase" or args[1] == "Buy" then
                        return true -- 拦截购买请求
                    end
                    return oldFire(remote, ...)
                end
                hookedRemotes[name] = true
            elseif remote:IsA("RemoteFunction") then
                local oldInvoke = remote.InvokeServer
                remote.InvokeServer = function(_, ...)
                    local args = {...}
                    if args[1] == "Purchase" or args[1] == "Buy" then
                        return true -- 拦截购买请求
                    end
                    return oldInvoke(remote, ...)
                end
                hookedRemotes[name] = true
            end
        end
    end
    
    Library:Notify("通行证系统", "已启用全局通行证权限")
end

local function disableGamepassHacks()
    -- 恢复原始UserId
    game.Players.LocalPlayer.UserId = originalUserId
    
    -- 恢复GamePassService方法
    local gamepassService = game:GetService("GamePassService")
    if originalPlayerHasPass then
        gamepassService.PlayerHasPass = originalPlayerHasPass
        originalPlayerHasPass = nil
    end
    
    -- 恢复所有被拦截的远程调用
    for name, _ in pairs(hookedRemotes) do
        local remote = game.ReplicatedStorage:FindFirstChild(name)
        if remote then
            if remote:IsA("RemoteEvent") then
                remote.FireServer = nil -- 恢复原始方法
            elseif remote:IsA("RemoteFunction") then
                remote.InvokeServer = nil -- 恢复原始方法
            end
        end
    end
    hookedRemotes = {}
    
    Library:Notify("通行证系统", "已禁用所有通行证修改")
end

superuniversal9:Toggle("伪管理员权限", "GlobalGamepass", false, function(state)
    gamepassEnabled = state
    if state then
        enableGamepassHacks()
        
        -- 确保角色重生后仍然保持效果
        game.Players.LocalPlayer.CharacterAdded:Connect(function()
            if gamepassEnabled then
                enableGamepassHacks()
            end
        end)
    else
        disableGamepassHacks()
    end
end)

-- 角色重生时重新应用效果
game.Players.LocalPlayer.CharacterAdded:Connect(function()
    if gamepassEnabled then
        enableGamepassHacks()
    end
end)

    if infiniteJumpEnabled then
        game:GetService"Players".LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChildOfClass'Humanoid':ChangeState("Jumping")
    end
end)

-- 行走播放动作功能变量
local emotesWalkEnabled = false
local currentEmoteTrack = nil
local currentCharacter = nil

-- 获取玩家服务
local Players = game:GetService("Players")
local player = Players.LocalPlayer

-- 停止当前表情动画
local function stopCurrentEmote()
    if currentEmoteTrack then
        currentEmoteTrack:Stop()
        currentEmoteTrack = nil
    end
end

-- 播放表情动画
local function playEmote(humanoid, emoteId)
    stopCurrentEmote()
    
    local animation = Instance.new("Animation")
    animation.AnimationId = "rbxassetid://" .. emoteId

    local success, animTrack = pcall(function()
        return humanoid.Animator:LoadAnimation(animation)
    end)

    if success and animTrack then
        currentEmoteTrack = animTrack
        currentEmoteTrack.Priority = Enum.AnimationPriority.Action
        currentEmoteTrack.Looped = true
        currentEmoteTrack:Play()
    end
end

-- 检测是否是表情动画
local function isDancing(character, animationTrack)
    if not character:FindFirstChild("Animate") then return false end
    
    local animationId = animationTrack.Animation.AnimationId
    
    -- 检查动画ID是否包含表情动画的特征
    if string.find(animationId, "emoji") or string.find(animationId, "emote") or string.find(animationId, "dance") then
        return true
    end
    
    -- 检查是否不在基础动画中
    for _, animationHolder in pairs(character.Animate:GetChildren()) do
        if animationHolder:IsA("StringValue") then
            for _, animation in pairs(animationHolder:GetChildren()) do
                if animation:IsA("Animation") and animation.AnimationId == animationId then
                    return false
                end
            end
        end
    end
    
    return true
end

-- 角色添加时设置事件监听
local function onCharacterAdded(character)
    currentCharacter = character
    stopCurrentEmote()

    local humanoid = character:WaitForChild("Humanoid")
    local animator = humanoid:WaitForChild("Animator")

    animator.AnimationPlayed:Connect(function(animationTrack)
        if isDancing(character, animationTrack) then
            local playedEmoteId = string.match(animationTrack.Animation.AnimationId, "%d+") -- 提取动画ID数字部分
            
            if playedEmoteId and emotesWalkEnabled then
                if currentEmoteTrack then
                    local currentEmoteId = string.match(currentEmoteTrack.Animation.AnimationId, "%d+")
                    if currentEmoteId == playedEmoteId then return end
                    stopCurrentEmote()
                end
                playEmote(humanoid, playedEmoteId)
            end
        end
    end)

    humanoid.Died:Connect(stopCurrentEmote)
end

-- 初始化角色监听
if player.Character then
    onCharacterAdded(player.Character)
end
player.CharacterAdded:Connect(onCharacterAdded)

-- 移动时处理表情
local RunService = game:GetService("RunService")
RunService.Stepped:Connect(function()
    if player.Character and player.Character:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") then
        local humanoid = player.Character.Humanoid
        if humanoid and currentEmoteTrack and currentEmoteTrack.IsPlaying then
            if humanoid.MoveDirection.Magnitude > 0 and not emotesWalkEnabled then
                stopCurrentEmote()
            end
        end
    end
end)

    superuniversal9:Toggle("行走播放动作(就是所有动画无法取消)", "EmoteWalk", false, function(state)
        emotesWalkEnabled = state
        Library:Notify("行走播放动作", state and "已启用" or "已禁用")
    end)
end

local Players = game:GetService("Players")
local RunService = game:GetService("RunService")

local player = Players.LocalPlayer
local character = player.Character or player.CharacterAdded:Wait()
local humanoid = character:WaitForChild("Humanoid")

local autoAttackEnabled = false
local attacking = false
local lastAttackTime = 0
local attackCooldown = 0.01 -- 更短的攻击冷却时间以提高攻击速度

-- 更通用的近战武器检测
local function isMeleeWeapon(tool)
    if not tool:FindFirstChild("Handle") then
        return false
    end
    
    -- 检查工具类型
    local toolType = tool:GetAttribute("ToolType") or ""
    if toolType:lower():find("melee") or toolType:lower():find("sword") or toolType:lower():find("weapon") then
        return true
    end
    
    -- 检查工具名称
    local name = tool.Name:lower()
    local meleeKeywords = {"sword", "knife", "axe", "bat", "hammer", "blade", "dagger", "mace", "club", "katana", "saber", "rapier"}
    
    for _, keyword in ipairs(meleeKeywords) do
        if name:find(keyword) then
            return true
        end
    end
    
    -- 检查工具描述
    local desc = tool:GetAttribute("Description") or ""
    for _, keyword in ipairs(meleeKeywords) do
        if desc:lower():find(keyword) then
            return true
        end
    end
    
    return false
end

-- 获取范围内的敌人（更通用的检测）
local function getEnemiesInRange(range)
    local enemies = {}
    local character = player.Character
    if not character then return enemies end
    
    local rootPart = character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
    if not rootPart then return enemies end
    
    -- 检测所有可能的目标（包括NPC）
    for _, obj in ipairs(workspace:GetChildren()) do
        if obj:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") and obj:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
            local objHumanoid = obj:FindFirstChild("Humanoid")
            local objRoot = obj:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
            
            -- 排除玩家自己的角色
            if obj ~= character and objHumanoid.Health > 0 then
                local distance = (rootPart.Position - objRoot.Position).Magnitude
                if distance <= range then
                    table.insert(enemies, {
                        object = obj,
                        humanoid = objHumanoid,
                        rootPart = objRoot,
                        distance = distance
                    })
                end
            end
        end
    end
    
    -- 检测其他玩家
    for _, otherPlayer in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
        if otherPlayer ~= player and otherPlayer.Character then
            local otherHumanoid = otherPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("Humanoid")
            local otherRoot = otherPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
            
            if otherHumanoid and otherHumanoid.Health > 0 and otherRoot then
                local distance = (rootPart.Position - otherRoot.Position).Magnitude
                if distance <= range then
                    table.insert(enemies, {
                        player = otherPlayer,
                        character = otherPlayer.Character,
                        humanoid = otherHumanoid,
                        rootPart = otherRoot,
                        distance = distance
                    })
                end
            end
        end
    end
    
    return enemies
end

-- 更通用的攻击执行方法
local function performAttack()
    if attacking or tick() - lastAttackTime < attackCooldown then
        return
    end
    
    attacking = true
    lastAttackTime = tick()
    
    local tool = character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Tool")
    if tool then
        -- 尝试多种攻击方式
        local attackMethods = {
            -- 方法1: 触发远程事件
            function()
                local remoteEvent = tool:FindFirstChildOfClass("RemoteEvent")
                if remoteEvent then
                    pcall(function()
                        remoteEvent:FireServer("Attack")
                    end)
                    return true
                end
                return false
            end,
            
            -- 方法2: 触发远程函数
            function()
                local remoteFunction = tool:FindFirstChildOfClass("RemoteFunction")
                if remoteFunction then
                    pcall(function()
                        remoteFunction:InvokeServer("Attack")
                    end)
                    return true
                end
                return false
            end,
            
            -- 方法3: 触发点击检测器
            function()
                local clickDetector = tool:FindFirstChildOfClass("ClickDetector")
                if clickDetector then
                    pcall(function()
                        -- 模拟鼠标点击
                        clickDetector.MaxActivationDistance = 0
                        wait()
                        clickDetector.MaxActivationDistance = 100
                    end)
                    return true
                end
                return false
            end,
            
            -- 方法4: 直接调用工具上的方法
            function()
                local attackFunc = tool:FindFirstChild("Attack") or tool:FindFirstChild("attack")
                if attackFunc and attackFunc:IsA("ModuleScript") then
                    pcall(function()
                        local attackModule = require(attackFunc)
                        if type(attackModule) == "table" and attackModule.Attack then
                            attackModule.Attack()
                        end
                    end)
                    return true
                end
                return false
            end,
            
            -- 方法5: 激活工具的动画
            function()
                local animateScript = tool:FindFirstChild("Animate") or character:FindFirstChild("Animate")
                if animateScript then
                    pcall(function()
                        -- 尝试触发攻击动画
                        for _, track in pairs(humanoid:GetPlayingAnimationTracks()) do
                            if track.Animation then
                                local animName = track.Animation.Name:lower()
                                if animName:find("attack") or animName:find("swing") then
                                    track:Play()
                                end
                            end
                        end
                    end)
                    return true
                end
                return false
            end
        }
        
        -- 尝试所有攻击方法直到有一个成功
        for _, method in ipairs(attackMethods) do
            if method() then
                break
            end
        end
    end
    
    -- 短暂延迟后重置攻击状态
    wait(0.1)
    attacking = false
end

-- 自动攻击主循环
local attackConnection
local function startAutoAttack()
    if attackConnection then
        attackConnection:Disconnect()
    end
    
    attackConnection = RunService.Heartbeat:Connect(function()
        if not autoAttackEnabled then return end
        
        local tool = character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Tool")
        if tool and isMeleeWeapon(tool) then
            -- 获取范围内的敌人
            local enemies = getEnemiesInRange(20) -- 20单位范围内
            
            -- 如果有敌人，执行攻击
            if #enemies > 0 then
                -- 找到最近的敌人
                table.sort(enemies, function(a, b)
                    return a.distance < b.distance
                end)
                
                local closestEnemy = enemies[1]
                
                -- 面向敌人
                local rootPart = character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                if rootPart and closestEnemy.rootPart then
                    humanoid:MoveTo(closestEnemy.rootPart.Position)
                    
                    -- 执行攻击
                    performAttack()
                end
            end
        end
    end)
end

-- 角色变化时重新获取引用
player.CharacterAdded:Connect(function(newChar)
    character = newChar
    humanoid = newChar:WaitForChild("Humanoid")
    
    -- 如果自动攻击已启用，重新启动循环
    if autoAttackEnabled then
        startAutoAttack()
    end
end)

-- 添加自动攻击开关到UI
superuniversal9:Toggle("自动近战攻击", "AutoMeleeAttack", false, function(Value)
    autoAttackEnabled = Value
    if Value then
        startAutoAttack()
        print("自动近战攻击已启用")
    else
        if attackConnection then
            attackConnection:Disconnect()
            attackConnection = nil
        end
        print("自动近战攻击已禁用")
    end
end)

superuniversal9:Button("躺下", function()
    local speaker = game.Players.LocalPlayer
local character = speaker.Character
if not character then return end

local humanoid = character:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("Humanoid")
if not humanoid then return end

-- 修复1：确保角色坐下前不在载具中
if humanoid.SeatPart then
    humanoid.Sit = false
    wait(0.5)
end

-- 修复2：强制坐下并旋转角色
humanoid.Sit = true
wait(0.1) -- 确保坐下动画开始

-- 修复3：更安全的旋转逻辑
if humanoid.RootPart then
    local currentCFrame = humanoid.RootPart.CFrame
    -- 使用更精确的旋转角度计算
    humanoid.RootPart.CFrame = currentCFrame * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(90), 0, 0)
end

-- 修复4：停止所有动画（保持原逻辑）
for _, v in ipairs(humanoid:GetPlayingAnimationTracks()) do
    v:Stop()
end

end)

BFD1:Button("超人飞行R6(其实就是游泳的动作)", function()
    local Players = game:GetService("Players")
local RunService = game:GetService("RunService")
local LocalPlayer = Players.LocalPlayer
local Camera = workspace.CurrentCamera

local PlayerGui = LocalPlayer:WaitForChild("PlayerGui")
local screenGui = Instance.new("ScreenGui")
screenGui.Name = "DeltaControlGui"
screenGui.ResetOnSpawn = false
screenGui.IgnoreGuiInset = true
screenGui.Parent = PlayerGui

local toggleButton = Instance.new("ImageButton")
toggleButton.Name = "FlyToggle"
toggleButton.Size = UDim2.new(0, 100, 0, 100)
toggleButton.Position = UDim2.new(0.5, -50, 0.5, -50)
toggleButton.Image = "rbxassetid://76316158972959"
toggleButton.BackgroundTransparency = 1
toggleButton.Draggable = true
toggleButton.Active = true
toggleButton.Parent = screenGui

local brakeButton = Instance.new("ImageButton")
brakeButton.Name = "BrakeButton"
brakeButton.Size = UDim2.new(0, 80, 0, 80)
brakeButton.Position = UDim2.new(0.5, -40, 0.5, 60)
brakeButton.Image = "rbxassetid://132411019634629"
brakeButton.BackgroundTransparency = 1
brakeButton.Visible = false
brakeButton.Active = true
brakeButton.Parent = screenGui

local active = false
local braking = false
local rotConn, flyConn, animTrack
local bodyVelocity

local function getCharacter()
    return LocalPlayer.Character or LocalPlayer.CharacterAdded:Wait()
end

local function getRoot()
    return getCharacter():WaitForChild("HumanoidRootPart")
end

local function getHumanoid()
    return getCharacter():FindFirstChildWhichIsA("Humanoid")
end

local function setTPWalk(state)
    if syn or getgenv then
        pcall(function()
            setfflag("tpwalk", state and "1" or "0")
        end)
    end
end

local function playFlyAnimation()
    local hum = getHumanoid()
    if hum then
        local anim = Instance.new("Animation")
        anim.AnimationId = "rbxassetid://282574440"
        animTrack = hum:LoadAnimation(anim)
        animTrack.Looped = true
        animTrack:Play()
    end
end

local function playBrakeAnimation()
    local hum = getHumanoid()
    if hum then
        local anim = Instance.new("Animation")
        anim.AnimationId = "rbxassetid://69427277"
        animTrack = hum:LoadAnimation(anim)
        animTrack.Looped = true
        animTrack:Play()
    end
end

local function stopAnimation()
    if animTrack then
        animTrack:Stop()
        animTrack = nil
    end
end

local function startFlying()
    local root = getRoot()
    bodyVelocity = Instance.new("BodyVelocity")
    bodyVelocity.Velocity = Vector3.zero
    bodyVelocity.MaxForce = Vector3.new(1e9, 1e9, 1e9)
    bodyVelocity.P = 1250
    bodyVelocity.Parent = root

    flyConn = RunService.RenderStepped:Connect(function()
        if not braking then
            local camLook = Camera.CFrame.LookVector
            bodyVelocity.Velocity = camLook * 50
        else
            bodyVelocity.Velocity = Vector3.zero
        end
    end)
end

local function stopFlying()
    if flyConn then
        flyConn:Disconnect()
        flyConn = nil
    end
    if bodyVelocity then
        bodyVelocity:Destroy()
        bodyVelocity = nil
    end
end

local function startRotation()
    rotConn = RunService.RenderStepped:Connect(function()
        local root = getRoot()
        if root then
            root.CFrame = CFrame.new(root.Position, root.Position + Camera.CFrame.LookVector)
        end
    end)
end

local function stopRotation()
    if rotConn then
        rotConn:Disconnect()
        rotConn = nil
    end
end

local function activate()
    active = true
    braking = false
    setTPWalk(true)
    playFlyAnimation()
    startFlying()
    startRotation()
    brakeButton.Visible = true
end

local function deactivate()
    active = false
    stopAnimation()
    stopFlying()
    stopRotation()
    setTPWalk(false)
    brakeButton.Visible = false
end

local function toggleBrake()
    braking = not braking
    stopAnimation()
    if braking then
        playBrakeAnimation()
    else
        playFlyAnimation()
    end
end

toggleButton.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
    if active then
        deactivate()
    else
        activate()
    end
end)

brakeButton.MouseButton1Click:Connect(toggleBrake)

LocalPlayer.CharacterAdded:Connect(function()
    if active then
        task.wait(1)
        activate()
        if braking then
            toggleBrake()
        end
    end
end)
end)

  loadstring(game:HttpGet("https://rawscripts.net/raw/Universal-Script-Invinicible-Flight-R15-45414"))()
end)

BFD1:Button("R15变R6", function()
--reanimate by MyWorld#4430 discord.gg/pYVHtSJmEY
--"oMg tHIs cODe iS uNReaDabLe sO iT SUckS" -its not a script for u to understand and edit but to use with your other scripts
local v3_net, v3_808 = Vector3.new(0, 25.1, 0), Vector3.new(8, 0, 8)
    local function getNetlessVelocity(realPartVelocity)
        local mag = realPartVelocity.Magnitude
        if mag > 1 then
            local unit = realPartVelocity.Unit
            if (unit.Y > 0.25) or (unit.Y < -0.75) then
                return unit * (25.1 / unit.Y)
            end
        end
        return v3_net + realPartVelocity * v3_808
    end
    local simradius = "shp" --simulation radius (net bypass) method
--"shp" - sethiddenproperty
--"ssr" - setsimulationradius
--false - disable
local simrad = 1000 --simulation radius value
local healthHide = true --moves your head away every 3 seconds so players dont see your health bar (alignmode 4 only)
local reclaim = true --if you lost control over a part this will move your primary part to the part so you get it back (alignmode 4)
local novoid = true --prevents parts from going under workspace.FallenPartsDestroyHeight if you control them (alignmode 4 only)
local physp = nil --PhysicalProperties.new(0.01, 0, 1, 0, 0) --sets .CustomPhysicalProperties to this for each part
local noclipAllParts = false --set it to true if you want noclip
local antiragdoll = true --removes hingeConstraints and ballSocketConstraints from your character
local newanimate = true --disables the animate script and enables after reanimation
local discharscripts = true --disables all localScripts parented to your character before reanimation
local R15toR6 = true --tries to convert your character to r6 if its r15
local hatcollide = true --makes hats cancollide (credit to ShownApe) (works only with reanimate method 0)
local humState16 = true --enables collisions for limbs before the humanoid dies (using hum:ChangeState)
local addtools = false --puts all tools from backpack to character and lets you hold them after reanimation
local hedafterneck = true --disable aligns for head and enable after neck or torso is removed
local loadtime = game:GetService("Players").RespawnTime + 100000 --anti respawn delay
local method = 3 --reanimation method
--methods:
--0 - breakJoints (takes [loadtime] seconds to load)
--1 - limbs
--2 - limbs + anti respawn
--3 - limbs + breakJoints after [loadtime] seconds
--4 - remove humanoid + breakJoints
--5 - remove humanoid + limbs
local alignmode = 4 --AlignPosition mode
--modes:
--1 - AlignPosition rigidity enabled true
--2 - 2 AlignPositions rigidity enabled both true and false
--3 - AlignPosition rigidity enabled false
--4 - no AlignPosition, CFrame only
local flingpart = "HumanoidRootPart" --name of the part or the hat used for flinging
--the fling function
--usage: fling(target, duration, velocity)
--target can be set to: basePart, CFrame, Vector3, character model or humanoid (flings at mouse.Hit if argument not provided)
--duration (fling time in seconds) can be set to a number or a string convertable to a number (0.5s if not provided)
--velocity (fling part rotation velocity) can be set to a vector3 value (Vector3.new(20000, 20000, 20000) if not provided)

local lp = game:GetService("Players").LocalPlayer
local rs, ws, sg = game:GetService("RunService"), game:GetService("Workspace"), game:GetService("StarterGui")
local stepped, heartbeat, renderstepped = rs.Stepped, rs.Heartbeat, rs.RenderStepped
local twait, tdelay, rad, inf, abs, clamp = task.wait, task.delay, math.rad, math.huge, math.abs, math.clamp
local cf, v3, angles = CFrame.new, Vector3.new, CFrame.Angles
local v3_0, cf_0 = v3(0, 0, 0), cf(0, 0, 0)

local c = lp.Character
if not (c and c.Parent) then
    return
end

c:GetPropertyChangedSignal("Parent"):Connect(function()
    if not (c and c.Parent) then
        c = nil
    end
end)

local clone, destroy, getchildren, getdescendants, isa = c.Clone, c.Destroy, c.GetChildren, c.GetDescendants, c.IsA

local function gp(parent, name, className)
    if typeof(parent) == "Instance" then
        for i, v in pairs(getchildren(parent)) do
            if (v.Name == name) and isa(v, className) then
                return v
            end
        end
    end
    return nil
end

local fenv = getfenv()

local shp = fenv.sethiddenproperty or fenv.set_hidden_property or fenv.set_hidden_prop or fenv.sethiddenprop
local ssr = fenv.setsimulationradius or fenv.set_simulation_radius or fenv.set_sim_radius or fenv.setsimradius or fenv.setsimrad or fenv.set_sim_rad

healthHide = healthHide and ((method == 0) or (method == 2) or (method == 3)) and gp(c, "Head", "BasePart")

local reclaim, lostpart = reclaim and c.PrimaryPart, nil

local function align(Part0, Part1)
    
    local att0 = Instance.new("Attachment")
    att0.Position, att0.Orientation, att0.Name = v3_0, v3_0, "att0_" .. Part0.Name
    local att1 = Instance.new("Attachment")
    att1.Position, att1.Orientation, att1.Name = v3_0, v3_0, "att1_" .. Part1.Name

    if alignmode == 4 then
    
        local hide = false
        if Part0 == healthHide then
            healthHide = false
            tdelay(0, function()
                while twait(2.9) and Part0 and c do
                    hide = #Part0:GetConnectedParts() == 1
                    twait(0.1)
                    hide = false
                end
            end)
        end
        
        local rot = rad(0.05)
        local con0, con1 = nil, nil
        con0 = stepped:Connect(function()
            if not (Part0 and Part1) then return con0:Disconnect() and con1:Disconnect() end
            Part0.RotVelocity = Part1.RotVelocity
        end)
        local lastpos = Part0.Position
        con1 = heartbeat:Connect(function(delta)
            if not (Part0 and Part1 and att1) then return con0:Disconnect() and con1:Disconnect() end
            if (not Part0.Anchored) and (Part0.ReceiveAge == 0) then
                if lostpart == Part0 then
                    lostpart = nil
                end
                local newcf = Part1.CFrame * att1.CFrame
                if Part1.Velocity.Magnitude > 0.1 then
                    Part0.Velocity = getNetlessVelocity(Part1.Velocity)
                else
                    local vel = (newcf.Position - lastpos) / delta
                    Part0.Velocity = getNetlessVelocity(vel)
                    if vel.Magnitude < 1 then
                        rot = -rot
                        newcf *= angles(0, 0, rot)
                    end
                end
                lastpos = newcf.Position
                if lostpart and (Part0 == reclaim) then
                    newcf = lostpart.CFrame
                elseif hide then
                    newcf += v3(0, 3000, 0)
                end
                if novoid and (newcf.Y < ws.FallenPartsDestroyHeight + 0.1) then
                    newcf += v3(0, ws.FallenPartsDestroyHeight + 0.1 - newcf.Y, 0)
                end
                Part0.CFrame = newcf
            elseif (not Part0.Anchored) and (abs(Part0.Velocity.X) < 45) and (abs(Part0.Velocity.Y) < 25) and (abs(Part0.Velocity.Z) < 45) then
                lostpart = Part0
            end
        end)
    
    else
        
        Part0.CustomPhysicalProperties = physp
        if (alignmode == 1) or (alignmode == 2) then
            local ape = Instance.new("AlignPosition")
            ape.MaxForce, ape.MaxVelocity, ape.Responsiveness = inf, inf, inf
            ape.ReactionForceEnabled, ape.RigidityEnabled, ape.ApplyAtCenterOfMass = false, true, false
            ape.Attachment0, ape.Attachment1, ape.Name = att0, att1, "AlignPositionRtrue"
            ape.Parent = att0
        end
        
        if (alignmode == 2) or (alignmode == 3) then
            local apd = Instance.new("AlignPosition")
            apd.MaxForce, apd.MaxVelocity, apd.Responsiveness = inf, inf, inf
            apd.ReactionForceEnabled, apd.RigidityEnabled, apd.ApplyAtCenterOfMass = false, false, false
            apd.Attachment0, apd.Attachment1, apd.Name = att0, att1, "AlignPositionRfalse"
            apd.Parent = att0
        end
        
        local ao = Instance.new("AlignOrientation")
        ao.MaxAngularVelocity, ao.MaxTorque, ao.Responsiveness = inf, inf, inf
        ao.PrimaryAxisOnly, ao.ReactionTorqueEnabled, ao.RigidityEnabled = false, false, false
        ao.Attachment0, ao.Attachment1 = att0, att1
        ao.Parent = att0
        
        local con0, con1 = nil, nil
        local vel = Part0.Velocity
        con0 = renderstepped:Connect(function()
            if not (Part0 and Part1) then return con0:Disconnect() and con1:Disconnect() end
            Part0.Velocity = vel
        end)
        local lastpos = Part0.Position
        con1 = heartbeat:Connect(function(delta)
            if not (Part0 and Part1) then return con0:Disconnect() and con1:Disconnect() end
            vel = Part0.Velocity
            if Part1.Velocity.Magnitude > 0.01 then
                Part0.Velocity = getNetlessVelocity(Part1.Velocity)
            else
                Part0.Velocity = getNetlessVelocity((Part0.Position - lastpos) / delta)
            end
            lastpos = Part0.Position
        end)
    
    end

    att0:GetPropertyChangedSignal("Parent"):Connect(function()
        Part0 = att0.Parent
        if not isa(Part0, "BasePart") then
            att0 = nil
            if lostpart == Part0 then
                lostpart = nil
            end
            Part0 = nil
        end
    end)
    att0.Parent = Part0
    
    att1:GetPropertyChangedSignal("Parent"):Connect(function()
        Part1 = att1.Parent
        if not isa(Part1, "BasePart") then
            att1 = nil
            Part1 = nil
        end
    end)
    att1.Parent = Part1
end

local function respawnrequest()
    local ccfr, c = ws.CurrentCamera.CFrame, lp.Character
    lp.Character = nil
    lp.Character = c
    local con = nil
    con = ws.CurrentCamera.Changed:Connect(function(prop)
        if (prop ~= "Parent") and (prop ~= "CFrame") then
            return
        end
        ws.CurrentCamera.CFrame = ccfr
        con:Disconnect()
    end)
end

local destroyhum = (method == 4) or (method == 5)
local breakjoints = (method == 0) or (method == 4)
local antirespawn = (method == 0) or (method == 2) or (method == 3)

hatcollide = hatcollide and (method == 0)

addtools = addtools and lp:FindFirstChildOfClass("Backpack")

if type(simrad) ~= "number" then simrad = 1000 end
if shp and (simradius == "shp") then
    tdelay(0, function()
        while c do
            shp(lp, "SimulationRadius", simrad)
            heartbeat:Wait()
        end
    end)
elseif ssr and (simradius == "ssr") then
    tdelay(0, function()
        while c do
            ssr(simrad)
            heartbeat:Wait()
        end
    end)
end

if antiragdoll then
    antiragdoll = function(v)
        if isa(v, "HingeConstraint") or isa(v, "BallSocketConstraint") then
            v.Parent = nil
        end
    end
    for i, v in pairs(getdescendants(c)) do
        antiragdoll(v)
    end
    c.DescendantAdded:Connect(antiragdoll)
end

if antirespawn then
    respawnrequest()
end

if method == 0 then
    twait(loadtime)
    if not c then
        return
    end
end

if discharscripts then
    for i, v in pairs(getdescendants(c)) do
        if isa(v, "LocalScript") then
            v.Disabled = true
        end
    end
elseif newanimate then
    local animate = gp(c, "Animate", "LocalScript")
    if animate and (not animate.Disabled) then
        animate.Disabled = true
    else
        newanimate = false
    end
end

if addtools then
    for i, v in pairs(getchildren(addtools)) do
        if isa(v, "Tool") then
            v.Parent = c
        end
    end
end

pcall(function()
    settings().Physics.AllowSleep = false
    settings().Physics.PhysicsEnvironmentalThrottle = Enum.EnviromentalPhysicsThrottle.Disabled
end)

local OLDscripts = {}

for i, v in pairs(getdescendants(c)) do
    if v.ClassName == "Script" then
        OLDscripts[v.Name] = true
    end
end

local scriptNames = {}

for i, v in pairs(getdescendants(c)) do
    if isa(v, "BasePart") then
        local newName, exists = tostring(i), true
        while exists do
            exists = OLDscripts[newName]
            if exists then
                newName = newName .. "_"    
            end
        end
        table.insert(scriptNames, newName)
        Instance.new("Script", v).Name = newName
    end
end

local hum = c:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
if hum then
    for i, v in pairs(hum:GetPlayingAnimationTracks()) do
        v:Stop()
    end
end
c.Archivable = true
local cl = clone(c)
if hum and humState16 then
    hum:ChangeState(Enum.HumanoidStateType.Physics)
    if destroyhum then
        twait(1.6)
    end
end
if destroyhum then
    pcall(destroy, hum)
end

if not c then
    return
end

local head, torso, root = gp(c, "Head", "BasePart"), gp(c, "Torso", "BasePart") or gp(c, "UpperTorso", "BasePart"), gp(c, "HumanoidRootPart", "BasePart")
if hatcollide then
    pcall(destroy, torso)
    pcall(destroy, root)
    pcall(destroy, c:FindFirstChildOfClass("BodyColors") or gp(c, "Health", "Script"))
end

local model = Instance.new("Model", c)
model:GetPropertyChangedSignal("Parent"):Connect(function()
    if not (model and model.Parent) then
        model = nil
    end
end)

for i, v in pairs(getchildren(c)) do
    if v ~= model then
        if addtools and isa(v, "Tool") then
            for i1, v1 in pairs(getdescendants(v)) do
                if v1 and v1.Parent and isa(v1, "BasePart") then
                    local bv = Instance.new("BodyVelocity")
                    bv.Velocity, bv.MaxForce, bv.P, bv.Name = v3_0, v3(1000, 1000, 1000), 1250, "bv_" .. v.Name
                    bv.Parent = v1
                end
            end
        end
        v.Parent = model
    end
end

if breakjoints then
    model:BreakJoints()
else
    if head and torso then
        for i, v in pairs(getdescendants(model)) do
            if isa(v, "JointInstance") then
                local save = false
                if (v.Part0 == torso) and (v.Part1 == head) then
                    save = true
                end
                if (v.Part0 == head) and (v.Part1 == torso) then
                    save = true
                end
                if save then
                    if hedafterneck then
                        hedafterneck = v
                    end
                else
                    pcall(destroy, v)
                end
            end
        end
    end
    if method == 3 then
        task.delay(loadtime, pcall, model.BreakJoints, model)
    end
end

cl.Parent = ws
for i, v in pairs(getchildren(cl)) do
    v.Parent = c
end
pcall(destroy, cl)

local uncollide, noclipcon = nil, nil
if noclipAllParts then
    uncollide = function()
        if c then
            for i, v in pairs(getdescendants(c)) do
                if isa(v, "BasePart") then
                    v.CanCollide = false
                end
            end
        else
            noclipcon:Disconnect()
        end
    end
else
    uncollide = function()
        if model then
            for i, v in pairs(getdescendants(model)) do
                if isa(v, "BasePart") then
                    v.CanCollide = false
                end
            end
        else
            noclipcon:Disconnect()
        end
    end
end
noclipcon = stepped:Connect(uncollide)
uncollide()

for i, scr in pairs(getdescendants(model)) do
    if (scr.ClassName == "Script") and table.find(scriptNames, scr.Name) then
        local Part0 = scr.Parent
        if isa(Part0, "BasePart") then
            for i1, scr1 in pairs(getdescendants(c)) do
                if (scr1.ClassName == "Script") and (scr1.Name == scr.Name) and (not scr1:IsDescendantOf(model)) then
                    local Part1 = scr1.Parent
                    if (Part1.ClassName == Part0.ClassName) and (Part1.Name == Part0.Name) then
                        align(Part0, Part1)
                        pcall(destroy, scr)
                        pcall(destroy, scr1)
                        break
                    end
                end
            end
        end
    end
end

for i, v in pairs(getdescendants(c)) do
    if v and v.Parent and (not v:IsDescendantOf(model)) then
        if isa(v, "Decal") then
            v.Transparency = 1
        elseif isa(v, "BasePart") then
            v.Transparency = 1
            v.Anchored = false
        elseif isa(v, "ForceField") then
            v.Visible = false
        elseif isa(v, "Sound") then
            v.Playing = false
        elseif isa(v, "BillboardGui") or isa(v, "SurfaceGui") or isa(v, "ParticleEmitter") or isa(v, "Fire") or isa(v, "Smoke") or isa(v, "Sparkles") then
            v.Enabled = false
        end
    end
end

if newanimate then
    local animate = gp(c, "Animate", "LocalScript")
    if animate then
        animate.Disabled = false
    end
end

if addtools then
    for i, v in pairs(getchildren(c)) do
        if isa(v, "Tool") then
            v.Parent = addtools
        end
    end
end

local hum0, hum1 = model:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid"), c:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
if hum0 then
    hum0:GetPropertyChangedSignal("Parent"):Connect(function()
        if not (hum0 and hum0.Parent) then
            hum0 = nil
        end
    end)
end
if hum1 then
    hum1:GetPropertyChangedSignal("Parent"):Connect(function()
        if not (hum1 and hum1.Parent) then
            hum1 = nil
        end
    end)

    ws.CurrentCamera.CameraSubject = hum1
    local camSubCon = nil
    local function camSubFunc()
        camSubCon:Disconnect()
        if c and hum1 then
            ws.CurrentCamera.CameraSubject = hum1
        end
    end
    camSubCon = renderstepped:Connect(camSubFunc)
    if hum0 then
        hum0:GetPropertyChangedSignal("Jump"):Connect(function()
            if hum1 then
                hum1.Jump = hum0.Jump
            end
        end)
    else
        respawnrequest()
    end
end

local rb = Instance.new("BindableEvent", c)
rb.Event:Connect(function()
    pcall(destroy, rb)
    sg:SetCore("ResetButtonCallback", true)
    if destroyhum then
        if c then c:BreakJoints() end
        return
    end
    if model and hum0 and (hum0.Health > 0) then
        model:BreakJoints()
        hum0.Health = 0
    end
    if antirespawn then
        respawnrequest()
    end
end)
sg:SetCore("ResetButtonCallback", rb)

tdelay(0, function()
    while c do
        if hum0 and hum1 then
            hum1.Jump = hum0.Jump
        end
        wait()
    end
    sg:SetCore("ResetButtonCallback", true)
end)

emoteNames = { wave = false, point = false, dance1 = true, dance2 = true, dance3 = true, laugh = false, cheer = false} local function configureAnimationSet(name, fileList) if (animTable[name] ~= nil) then for _, connection in pairs(animTable[name].connections) do connection:disconnect() end end animTable[name] = {} animTable[name].count = 0 animTable[name].totalWeight = 0 animTable[name].connections = {} local config = script:FindFirstChild(name) if (config ~= nil) then table.insert(animTable[name].connections, config.ChildAdded:connect(function(child) configureAnimationSet(name, fileList) end)) table.insert(animTable[name].connections, config.ChildRemoved:connect(function(child) configureAnimationSet(name, fileList) end)) local idx = 1 for _, childPart in pairs(config:GetChildren()) do if (childPart:IsA("Animation")) then table.insert(animTable[name].connections, childPart.Changed:connect(function(property) configureAnimationSet(name, fileList) end)) animTable[name][idx] = {} animTable[name][idx].anim = childPart local weightObject = childPart:FindFirstChild("Weight") if (weightObject == nil) then animTable[name][idx].weight = 1 else animTable[name][idx].weight = weightObject.Value end animTable[name].count = animTable[name].count + 1 animTable[name].totalWeight = animTable[name].totalWeight + animTable[name][idx].weight idx = idx + 1 end end end if (animTable[name].count <= 0) then for idx, anim in pairs(fileList) do animTable[name][idx] = {} animTable[name][idx].anim = Instance.new("Animation") animTable[name][idx].anim.Name = name animTable[name][idx].anim.AnimationId = anim.id animTable[name][idx].weight = anim.weight animTable[name].count = animTable[name].count + 1 animTable[name].totalWeight = animTable[name].totalWeight + anim.weight end end end local function scriptChildModified(child) local fileList = animNames[child.Name] if (fileList ~= nil) then
